Patch #2141 has been updated. 

Project: destar
Category: None
Status: Open
Submitted by: tzafrir
Assigned to : none
Summary: asterisk 1.4/iax phone misbehaves with empty defaultip

Follow-Ups:

Date: 2007-Aug-14 00:38
By: tzafrir

Comment:
An IAX2 phone defined in Asterisk 1.4 should not have a defaultip= line with an empty value. This will cause the phone's entry to be ignored.

Fix: just don't write that line if the value is empty (and hence useless anyway).
-------------------------------------------------------

-------------------------------------------------------

--- trunk/page_user_phonebook.ptl	2007-08-14 05:48:25 UTC (rev 786)
+++ trunk/page_user_phonebook.ptl	2007-08-14 06:00:09 UTC (rev 787)
@@ -0,0 +1,61 @@
+# -*- coding: iso-latin-1 -*-
+#
+# Copyright (C) 2005 by Holger Schurig
+# 
+# This program is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify
+# it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
+# the Free Software Foundation; either version 2 of the License, or
+# (at your option) any later version.
+#
+# This program is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
+# but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
+# MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
+# GNU General Public License for more details.
+#
+# You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
+# along with this program; if not, write to the Free Software
+# Foundation, Inc., 59 Temple Place, Suite 330, Boston, MA  02111-1307  USA
+#
+
+
+from Templates import *
+from quixote.directory import Directory, AccessControlled
+from quixote import get_request, get_session, redirect
+import backend, manager, configlets
+import time,types
+
+class Page(AccessControlled, Directory): 
+
+
+	_q_parent  = 'page_user'
+	_q_title   = _("Phones List")
+	_q_desc    = _("All Phones and Shortcuts")
+	_q_link    = 'phoneslist'
+	_q_menupos = 10
+	_q_level   = 1
+
+	_q_exports = ['']
+
+	def _q_access(self):
+		self.session = get_session()
+		self.request = get_request()
+		if self.session.level < self._q_level:
+			cantAccessPage()
+
+
+	def _q_index [plain] (self):
+		header(self._q_desc)
+        
+		'<h3>Phones</h3>'
+		'<table>'
+		'<tr><th>Number</th> <th>Short Name</th> <th>Name</th></tr>'
+		for o in backend.getConfiglets('Phones'):
+			if self.session.pbx:
+				if o.pbx == self.session.pbx:
+					'<tr><td>%s</td> <td>%s</td> <td>%s</td></tr>' % (o.ext, o.shortName, o.name)
+			else:
+				'<tr><td>%s</td> <td>%s</td> <td>%s</td></tr>' % (o.ext, o.shortName, o.name)
+		'</table>'
+		
+		footer()
+

@@ -0,0 +1,54 @@
+# -*- coding: iso-latin-1 -*-
+#
+# Copyright (C) 2005 by Holger Schurig
+# 
+# This program is free software; you can redistribute it and/or modify
+# it under the terms of the GNU General Public License as published by
+# the Free Software Foundation; either version 2 of the License, or
+# (at your option) any later version.
+#
+# This program is distributed in the hope that it will be useful,
+# but WITHOUT ANY WARRANTY; without even the implied warranty of
+# MERCHANTABILITY or FITNESS FOR A PARTICULAR PURPOSE.  See the
+# GNU General Public License for more details.
+#
+# You should have received a copy of the GNU General Public License
+# along with this program; if not, write to the Free Software
+# Foundation, Inc., 59 Temple Place, Suite 330, Boston, MA  02111-1307  USA
+#
+
+
+from Templates import *
+from quixote.directory import Directory, AccessControlled
+from quixote import get_request, get_session, redirect
+import backend, manager, configlets
+import time,types
+
+class Page(AccessControlled, Directory): 
+
+
+	_q_parent  = 'page_user'
+	_q_title   = '' 
+	_q_desc    = _("dial a phone")
+	_q_link    = 'dial'
+	_q_menupos = 3
+	_q_level   = 1
+
+	_q_exports = ['']
+
+	def _q_access(self):
+		self.session = get_session()
+		self.request = get_request()
+		if self.session.level < self._q_level:
+			cantAccessPage()
+
+	def _q_lookup(self, component):
+		if component:
+			if self.session.phone:
+				phone = backend.getConfiglet(name=self.session.phone)
+				manager.originateCallExt("%s/%s" % (phone.technology, phone.name), "out-%s" % phone.name, component, "1")
+				return redirect("../")
+			else:
+				return errorpage(_("You don't have an associated phone"))
+		else:
+			return errorpage(_("No destination number"))

Priority: 5
Submitted by: ffl
Assigned to : none
Summary: Sipgate needs "fromuser" in sip.conf

Details: To make a Sipgate.de trunk work we need "fromuser = SipgateID" in sip.conf. Otherwise this error occurs:
"wrong password on authentication for INVITE to ...."

<                       c.append("fromuser=%s" % self.id)

Now it "works for me".
